Except English (I) and English (II), Students are required to obtain 6 credits from 3 different thematic courses before graduation. The “English Testing” course is provided to students who fail to score 350 in a TOEIC mock held in the end of their first academic year. They will need to take the exam again after the course and pass; otherwise, they will need to take another “English Testing” course next semester.</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>全全民國防教育軍事訓練課程-國際情勢All-Out Defense Education and Researching of Military- International Situations (0)</p></td><td><p>全民國防教育軍事訓練課程-國際情勢All-Out Defense Education and Researching of Military- All-Out Defense (0)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education </p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術﹑自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四領域中各選修兩學分課程，共計8學分，其餘2學分學生可自由選擇，由通識講座課程、微課自主學習或通識四大領域課程中選課。惟按所屬院（系）之不同，學生選修四大領域課程時需符合以下規定：The General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a two-credit course from each category to get eight credits before graduation. The rest two credits can be chosen from the General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit and Self-Study course or four categories upon their needs.However, there are rules and limitations set by each college for taking a course from the four categories：</p><table><tr><td><p>(系)院</p><p>(Dept.)College</p></td><td><p>選課規定</p><p>Course requirements</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>中語系、應外系、藝設系與<strong>資傳系</strong></p><p>Dept. of Information Communication</p></td><td><p>不得再選人文領域(LE)，<strong>須於自然(GN), 生命(LS),社會(GS)三領域中選課</strong></p><p>General Education courses in the area of LE are not required; please select the courses from the areas of GN, LS or GS.</p></td></tr></table></td></tr></table>

</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>網站設計專題</p><p>Special Topics in Website Design</p><p>IC343</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>資訊安全</p><p>Information Programming</p><p>IC345</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共33學分外，本系必修科目為38學分，設計組必修27學分、科技組必修30學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修5學分，最低畢業學分為130學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】為本系設計組申請雙主修和輔系之先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為雙主修或輔系。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to “Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List” for general education course information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (33 credits), students must complete department required courses (38 credits) and group required courses (27 credits for Design group or 30 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and at least 5 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 130 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)".</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF05 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**Department of Information Communication, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2023)**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on April 29, 2026

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>(2)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>(2)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing (1)、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education (0)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education (0)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education (0)</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education (0)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。</p><p>Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共27學分外、院必修程式語言課程共4學分，本系必修科目為29學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修18學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (27 credits), College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, students must complete department required courses (29 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 18 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>5. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>6. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>7. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>8. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics Design” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>10. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department. </p><p>11. The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

Please refer to “Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List” for general education course information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (33 credits), students must complete department required courses (38 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 24→21 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)".</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. "Field Study (II)" (Course code IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming”(IC186) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p></td></tr></table>

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.	</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Design</p><p>IC343</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td><p>虛擬實境</p><p>Virtual Reality </p><p>IC346</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td><p>演算法</p><p>Algorithm</p><p>IC239</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共31學分外，本系必修科目為38學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修21學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】為本系設計組申請雙主修和輔系之先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為雙主修或輔系。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to “Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List” for general education course information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (31 credits), students must complete department required courses (38 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 21 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)".</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. "Field Study (II)" (Course code IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10.“Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming”(IC186), “Computer Graphics”(IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>11.To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

</p><p>IC346</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共31學分外，本系必修科目為35學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修21學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】為本系設計組申請雙主修和輔系之先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為雙主修或輔系。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (31 credits), students must complete department required courses (35 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 21 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>11. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</li></ol><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</li></ol><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。</p><p>Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic </p><p>IC346</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共31學分外，本系必修科目為32學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修21學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】為本系設計組申請雙主修和輔系之先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為雙主修或輔系。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (31 credits), students must complete department required courses (35 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 21 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>11. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF05 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

(II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing (1)、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education (0)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education (0)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education (0)</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education (0)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。</p><p>Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共27學分外、院必修程式語言課程共4學分，本系必修科目為29學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修18學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (27 credits), College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, students must complete department required courses (29 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 18 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>5. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>6. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>7. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>8. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics Design” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>10. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department. </p><p>11. The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

</p><p>IC346</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共31學分外，本系必修科目為35學分，設計組必修24學分、科技組必修21學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修12學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】為本系設計組申請雙主修和輔系之先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為雙主修或輔系。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (31 credits), students must complete department required courses (35 credits) and group required courses (24 credits for Design group or 21 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 12 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for double majors/minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their double majors/minor application is approved.</p><p>5. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>6. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>7. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>8. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>9. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>11. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

colspan="16"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程 10 學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> <strong>英語檢定English Testing （2）</strong>、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。</p><p>General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。</p><p>Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic <table><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共27學分外、院必修程式語言課程共4學分，本系必修科目為29學分，設計組必修18學分、科技組必修12學分。所屬組別的選修至少選修18學分(含系共同選修)，他組選修或他組必修至少選修6學分，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【數位影像處理】(IC120)、【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)、【3D電腦繪圖】(IC335)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (27 credits), College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, students must complete department required courses (29 credits) and group required courses (18 credits for Design group or 12 credits for Technology group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 18 credits based on their respective group (which include the department elective courses) and and at least 6 credits of required or elective courses from the other group. The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>5. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>6. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>7. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>8. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. “Digital Image Processing “(IC120), “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics Design” (IC205), ”Windows Programming” (IC238), “3D Computer Graphics” (IC335) are courses of 'digital application courses'.</p><p>10. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department. </p><p>11. The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF05 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.<strong> </strong>The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). <table><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>除共同必修科目及通識科目共27學分外、院必修程式語言課程共4學分，本系必修科目為29學分，數位媒體設計組必修9學分/智慧科技應用組必修12學分，系選修至少39學分，自由選修至多承認17學分 (含專業自主學習至多3學分)，最低畢業學分為128學分。</li><li>【藝術基礎一：素描】（3）與【藝術基礎二：創意素描】（3），上課時數皆為4小時。</li><li>修習專業實習課程須遵照專業實習辦法之相關規定。</li><li>選修本系碩士班課程可列入系選修學分。</li><li>終端學習課程：【專題製作二】(IC465)。</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li><li>【專題製作二】(IC465)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」。</li><li>【網頁程式設計】(IC186)、【電腦繪圖】(IC205)、【視窗應用程式設計】(IC238)、【3D電腦繪圖】(IC335)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」。</li><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>1. Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2. In addition to the university required and general education courses (27 credits), College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, students must complete department required courses (29 credits) and group required courses (9 credits for Digital Media Design Group or 9 credits for Intelligent Technology Group). For elective courses, students must complete at least 39 credits. A maximum of 17 credits can be recognized for free electives (including up to 3 credits for Disciplinary self-directed learning). The minimum graduation requirement is 128 credits in total.</p><p>3. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" and "Fundamentals of Arts (II)" courses are 4-hour classes with 3 credits.</p><p>4. Students taking the “Internship” course have to satisfy its regulations.</p><p>5. Department master courses can be counted as credits for department elective courses.</p><p>6. The experiential learning course: "Field Study (II)" (IC465).</p><p>7. The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>8. "Field Study (II)" (IC465) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. “Web Programming” (IC186), “Computer Graphics Design” (IC205),”Windows Programming”(IC238), “3D Computer Graphics” (IC335) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'.</p><p>10. To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department. </p><p>11. The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>12. Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

## 備註：

1.必修科目共計12學分。

2.〝藝術基礎I〞為輔系先修課程，須先修過此課程，系上始根據課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本系為輔系。

3.選擇本系為輔系之學生必須修滿24學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

4.本系課程設有擋修限制。

3. 選擇本系數位媒體設計組為輔系之學生必須修滿30學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。  
4. 本系課程設有擋修限制。

l 【藝術基礎I】為本系數位媒體設計組申請輔系先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系。

l 本系課程設有擋修限制。

基礎I】課程(於上學期開設)à 系上將根據【藝術基礎I】課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系à通過後始可開始選修課程。

106.04.26 一○五學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on April 26, 2017

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂

備註：

# 1 必修科目共計18學分。

# 2 【藝術基礎(一)：素描】為本系設計組申請輔系先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系。

# 3 選擇本系設計組為輔系之學生必須修滿30學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Remarks:

1. Required courses are 18 credits in total.
2. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their minor application is approved.
3. To qualify for the minor in Information Communication Design group, students must complete at least 30 credits.

## 請依學校輔系申請時程向系辦提出申請  準備作品集(含成績單)及參加口試  通過則可先修【藝術基礎(一)：素描】課程(於上學期開設)  系上將根據【藝術基礎(一)：素描】課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系  通過後始可開始選修課程。

2. 【藝術基礎(一)：素描】為本系設計組申請輔系先修課程，系上將根據該課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系。
3. 選擇本系設計組為輔系之學生必須修滿30學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Remarks:

1. Required courses are 18 credits in total.
2. "Fundamentals of Arts (I)" is the preparatory course for students applying for minor in the Design group and their performance in this course will determine if their minor application is approved.
3. To qualify for the minor in Information Communication Design group, students must complete at least 30 credits.

※依學校時程每學年第一學期期初向系辦提出申請準備作品集(含成績單)及參加口試通過則可先修【藝術基礎(一)：素描】課程(於上學期開設) 系上將根據【藝術基礎(一)：素描】課堂表現審核是否同意該生選修本組為輔系通過後始可開始選修課程。

※**Submit an application to the department office at the beginning of the fall semester according to the school schedule. Prepare a portfolio (including transcripts) and attend an oral exam. If passed, you may take the course "Fundamentals of Arts(I): Drawing" (only offered in the fall semester). The department will review the student's performance in "Fundamentals of Arts(I): Drawing" to decide whether to approve the student to choose this group as a minor. After approval, the student may begin selecting courses.**

1. 選擇本系設計組為輔系之學生必須修滿20學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Remarks:

1. To qualify for the minor in Information Communication Design group, students must complete at least 20 credits.

※ 請依學校時程提出申請準備作品集(含成績單) 遞交資傳系辦進行輔系資格審核通過後始可開始選修輔系課程。

※ **Please submit your application according to the school schedule.  Prepare a portfolio (including transcripts) and submit it to the Department of Information Communication for minor qualification review.  After approval, you may begin selecting minor courses.**

AA-CP-04-CF09 (1.3 版)／104.01.06 修訂

備註：

1. 選擇本系科技組為輔系之學生必須修滿20學分(含)以上，才予承認其輔系資格。
2. 修【IC184程式設計(一)】需同時加修【IC286程式設計實習(一)(0)】；【IC192程式設計(二)】需同時加修【IC200程式設計實習(二)(0)】。

Remarks:

1. To qualify for the minor in Information Communication Technology group, students must complete at least-20 credits.
2. "IC184\_Computer Programming (I)" and "IC286\_Computer Programming Lab. (I) (0)" must be taken concurrently. "IC192\_Computer Programming (II)" and "IC200\_Computer Programming Lab. (II) (0)" must be taken concurrently.

※ 請依學校時程提出申請準備作品集(含成績單) 遞交資傳系辦進行輔系資格審核通過後始可開始選修輔系課程。

※ **Please submit your application according to the school schedule.  Prepare a portfolio (including transcripts) and submit it to the Department of Information Communication for minor qualification review.  After approval, you may begin selecting minor courses.**

This course must be completed before students can apply for the oral examination of their master thesis.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

This course must be completed before students can apply for the oral examination of their master thesis.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年(Year)</p><p>學期(Semester)</p><p>科目(Course)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p><p>1<sup>st</sup> Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p><p>2<sup>nd</sup> Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester </p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td><td><p>上學期</p><p>Fall Semester </p></td><td><p>下學期</p><p>Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Required Courses</p><p>(7)</p></td><td><p>書報討論(一)</p><p>Seminar on Research Projects (I)</p><p>(1)</p><p>GI525</p></td><td><p>書報討論(二)</p><p>Seminar on Research Projects (II)</p><p>(1)</p><p>GI516</p></td><td><p>書報討論(三)</p><p>Seminar on Research Projects (III)</p><p>(1)</p><p>GI604</p></td><td><p>書報討論(四)</p><p>Seminar on Research Projects (IV)</p><p>(1)</p><p>GI629</p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>研究方法</p><p>Research Methodology</p><p>(3)</p><p>GI503</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學分小計</p><p>Credits Per Semester</p></td><td><p>1</p></td><td><p>4</p></td><td><p>1</p></td><td><p>1</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備 註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業計 24 學分+ 2～4學分（書報討論）+ 碩士論文6學分</li><li>每學期必須修讀並通過本所所開之書報討論課程（至多四學期）</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成<strong>學術研究倫理教育課程</strong>，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>The minimum graduation requirement is 24 credits in total, excluding graduate seminar (2-4 credits) and master thesis (6 credits).</li><li>Students must complete the graduate seminar which is a required course for four semesters.</li><li>Students must complete the Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first semester to satisfy the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. This course must be completed before students can apply for the oral examination of their master thesis.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

must complete at least 6 department elective courses before graduation.</li><li>Foreign students must complete elective courses with 24 credits approved by their thesis advisor.</li><li>Students must satisfy the regulations on academic publications before proceeding with the oral examination of their theses. (Please refer to “Regulations on Graduate Student Academic Publication in the Graduate School of Information Communication at Yuan Ze University” for more details.)</li><li>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</li></ol></td></tr></table>
